[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIssue  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring an interactive libFuzzer run of the `exif_from_data_fuzzer` harness, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer reported a one-byte heap-buffer-overflow in `exif_get_slong` at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`libexif/exif-utils.[0m[1;92mc:137:36[0m[39m`. The fuzzer invocation was:[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  run_fuzzer exif_from_data_fuzzer -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMemory Corruption Details  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow read occurred at address `[0m[1;36m0x50600000011f[0m[39m`, which is [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes past the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mend of a [0m[1;36m56[0m[39m-byte heap allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x[0m[39m…e0, [0m[1;36m0x[0m[39m…[0m[1;36m18[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The buffer was allocated via `malloc` inside the fuzzer driver.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow happens when interpreting data from a malformed input, specifically [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the Fuji maker-note parsing routine.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVulnerability Type  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Heap-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout-of-bounds read[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Classified by AddressSanitizer with [0m[33mSCARINESS[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m12[0m[39m for a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte heap overread.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The faulty read is performed by `exif_get_slong`, which reads a signed [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m-bit [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalue from a data pointer without sufficiently checking remaining buffer length.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error propagates through the Fuji-specific maker-note loader, suggesting the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue resides in the parsing of maker-note entries rather than the harness itself. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer environment was set to “interactive” mode with libFuzzer engine and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseed skipping enabled; only one input was tested [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m times, consistently [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproducing the overflow.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_get_long`, `exif_get_ulong`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- libexif/exif-data.c: Examine how overall EXIF data is loaded, especially the [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- exif_from_data_fuzzer.cc: While not the root cause, verify how test inputs are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed into `exif_data_new_from_data` to ensure the harness isn’t masking other [0m    [2m                [0m
